\\n113: ## About RBAC\\n114: \\n115: Role-based access control (RBAC) provides a standardized way of granting, changing, and revoking access so that users can view and modify Grafana resources, such *authn.Request) error {\n274: \tctx, span := s.tracer.Start(ctx, \"user.sync.SyncUserHook\")\n275: \tdefer span.End()\n276: \n277: \tif !id.ClientParams.SyncUser {\n278: \t\treturn nil\n279: \t}\n280: user\n295: \t\tusr, err = s.createUser(ctx, id)\n296: \n297: \t\t// There is a possibility for a race condition when creating a user. Most clients will probably not hit this\n298: \t\t// case but others will. The one we have seen this issue for is auth proxy. First time a new user loads grafana\n299: \t\t// several requests can get \"user.ErrUserNotFound\" at the same time but only one of the request will be allowed\n300: \t\t// to actually create the user, resulting in all other requests getting \"user.ErrUserAlreadyExists\". \t\t}\n305: \n306: \t\tif err != nil {\n307: \t\t\ts.log.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to create user\", \"error\", err, \"auth_module\", id.AuthenticatedBy, \"auth_id\", id.AuthID)\n308: `SyncUserHook` and `FetchSyncedUserHook` coordinate user data sync and populate teams\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/org_sync.go` - `SyncOrgRolesHook` handles organization role assignment from identity providers\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/rbac_sync.go` - `SyncPermissionsHook` fetches and applies RBAC permissions\\n- `pkg/services/authn/identity.go` - Core `Identity` struct with `Groups` field (IdP groups) and `Teams` field (assigned Grafana teams)\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authn.go` - `ClientParams` struct defines `SyncTeams` and `SyncOrgRoles` flags\\n\\n## Folder Permission Inheritance\\nFolder-level permissions are inherited by dashboards within them:\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go` - `GetInheritedScopes()` function retrieves inherited permission scopes from parent folders\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go` - Folder service that checks inherited permissions during folder access\\n- `pkg/api/folder.go` - `Evaluate()` method performs actual permission checks against user permissions\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go` - `Permission` (role-action-scope binding) and `ResourcePermission` models\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go` - `SetUserResourcePermission()` and team/role permission management\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go` - `getUserTeams()` retrieves teams for a user and their inherited permissions\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/store/queries.go` - Low-level SQL queries for permission resolution\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/iam/resourcepermission/sql.go` - Resource permission SQL backend\\n\\n## Permission Flow\\nWhen a user authenticates:\\n1. Identity provider groups are extracted into `Identity.Groups`\\n2. `SyncUserHook` creates/updates the user and `FetchSyncedUserHook` populates `Identity.Teams` with assigned teams\\n3. `SyncOrgRolesHook` assigns org-level roles from IdP org role mappings\\n4. `SyncPermissionsHook` loads user permissions via RBAC service\\n5. `AccessControl.Evaluate()` checks permissions using action-scope pairs\\n6. For folders/dashboards, `GetInheritedScopes()` includes parent folder permissions\\n7. hierarchy in Grafana is implemented across multiple interdependent services. Here's how they work together:\\n\\n## OrgUser Role Assignment\\nThe core organization user management is defined in `pkg/services/org/model.go` with the `OrgUser` struct representing an organization membership record. The assignment process is handled through:\\n- `pkg/services/org/orgimpl/store.go` - Contains `InsertOrgUser`, `AddOrgUser`, and `UpdateOrgUser` functions that manage org user database operations\\n- `pkg/api/org_users.go` - HTTP API endpoints for managing organization users and their roles\\n\\n## Team Management and Sync\\nTeam functionality is implemented in:\\n- `pkg/services/team/model.go` - Defines `Team` and `TeamMember` structures\\n- `pkg/services/team/teamimpl/team.go` - Team service implementation\\n- `pkg/services/team/teamimpl/store.go` - Database operations including `AddOrUpdateTeamMemberHook` and `RemoveTeamMemberHook` for team membership changes\\n- `pkg/services/team/teamapi/team_members.go` - HTTP API for team member management with support for both manual and LDAP-synced members\\n\\n## Team/Group Synchronization from Identity Providers\\nThe team synchronization from external identity providers is handled through:\\n- `pkg/services/ldap/ldap_groups.go` - Defines the `Groups` interface with `GetTeams()` method that maps LDAP groups to Grafana teams\\n- `pkg/services/ldap/ldap.go` - LDAP user and group retrieval logic\\n- `pkg/services/ldap/api/service.go` - API endpoint for syncing users with LDAP, including team membership\\n- `pkg/services/authn/clients/ldap.go` - LDAP authentication client that populates `Identity.Groups` from LDAP group memberships\\n- `pkg/services/authn/clients/oauth.go` - OAuth2 client that extracts groups from OAuth2 tokens\\n- `pkg/services/authn/clients/proxy.go` - Auth proxy client that reads groups from proxy headers\\n\\n## Identity Synchronization Hooks\\nThe identity synchronization pipeline manages both user and team sync:\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/user_sync.go` - `SyncUserHook` and `FetchSyncedUserHook` coordinate user data sync and populate teams\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/org_sync.go` - `SyncOrgRolesHook` handles organization role assignment from identity providers\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/rbac_sync.go` - `SyncPermissionsHook` fetches and applies RBAC permissions\\n- `pkg/services/authn/identity.go` - Core `Identity` struct with `Groups` field (IdP groups) and `Teams` field (assigned Grafana teams)\\n- `pkg/services/authn/authn.go` - `ClientParams` struct defines `SyncTeams` and `SyncOrgRoles` flags\\n\\n## Folder Permission Inheritance\\nFolder-level permissions are inherited by dashboards within them:\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go` - `GetInheritedScopes()` function retrieves inherited permission scopes from parent folders\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go` - Folder service that checks inherited permissions during folder access\\n- `pkg/api/folder.go` - HTTP API for folder management with permission evaluation\\n- `pkg/api/folder_permission.go` - Folder permission endpoints\\n\\n## RBAC Fine-Grained Permission Evaluation\\nThe RBAC permission evaluation engine is implemented in:\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go` - `AccessControl` interface for permission checks and `Service` interface for role management\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go` - `Evaluator` type that constructs permission evaluation expressions with AND/OR logic\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/access_control.go` - `Evaluate()` method performs actual permission checks against user permissions\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go` - `Permission` (role-action-scope binding) and `ResourcePermission` models\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go` - `SetUserResourcePermission()` and team/role permission management\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go` - `getUserTeams()` retrieves teams for a user and their inherited permissions\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/store/queries.go` - Low-level SQL queries for permission resolution\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/iam/resourcepermission/sql.go` - Resource permission SQL backend\\n\\n## Permission Flow\\nWhen a user authenticates:\\n1. Identity provider groups are extracted into `Identity.Groups`\\n2. `SyncUserHook` creates/updates the user and `FetchSyncedUserHook` populates `Identity.Teams` with assigned teams\\n3. `SyncOrgRolesHook` assigns org-level roles from IdP org role mappings\\n4. `SyncPermissionsHook` loads user permissions via RBAC service\\n5. `AccessControl.Evaluate()` checks permissions using action-scope pairs\\n6. For folders/dashboards, `GetInheritedScopes()` includes parent folder permissions\\n7. RBAC service resolves team memberships and applies role-based permissions\\n\\nThis hierarchy ensures that users inherit permissions through organizations, teams, and folder inheritance, while RBAC provides fine-grained control over individual actions on resources.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
